{"step_index":118,"source":"MODEL","type":"PLANNER_RESPONSE","status":"DONE","created_at":"2026-05-15T13:51:28Z","content":"I've completed the investigation and implemented the fixes for the website lagging, stem upload issues, and external file support.\n\n### Summary of Fixes:\n\n1.  **Website Lag Resolved:**\n    *   **Throttled Background Tasks:** The system no longer checks for winners or cleans up sold beats on every single page load. For large stems, this was causing massive lag.
